# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
Using a minimal number of annotations, markup the code below to successfully initialize the Spring Core Container.
You need to choose the semantically most appropriate annotation for the class. Note: if there are two fields somewhere and you think one should be 
"none of the above" then choose this option for the second field. If there are 2 annotations, 
sort them by name in ascending order

[@Configuration]
class Config {
        [@Bean][@Profile("x1")]
        public X x1() {
                // return x1 instance of X
        }
        [@Bean][@Profile("x2")]
        public X x2() {
                // return x2 instance of X
        }
}
[@Component]
class ServiceUsingX1 {
        [@Autowired]
        private Repository repository;
        [@Autowired]
        [@Qualifier("x1")]
        private X x;
        // ...
}
[@Component]
class ServiceUsingX2 {
        [@Autowired]
        private Repository repository;
        [@Autowired]
        [@Qualifier("x2")]
        private X x;

         public ServiceUsingX2([@Autowired]Repository repository,[@Autowired]X x) {
                // ...
        }
        // ...
}
[@Repository]
class Repository {
        // ...
}

Options:
[@Bean][@Profile("x1")][@Qualifier("x1")][@Configuration][@Qualifier("x2")][@ComponentScan]
[@Controller][@Autowired]
[@Profile("x2")][@Service][none of the above options][@Component][@Repository] ^12DNUbhP
